<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
使用 Markdown<a target="_blank" href="http://blog.leanote.com/post/freewalk/Markdown-%E8%AF%AD%E6%B3%95%E6%89%8B%E5%86%8C#fn:1" id="fnref:1" title="See footnote" class="footnote" style="color:red; text-decoration:none; word-wrap:break-word; background:transparent">1</a>可以效率的书写文档,
 直接转换成 HTML<a target="_blank" href="http://blog.leanote.com/post/freewalk/Markdown-%E8%AF%AD%E6%B3%95%E6%89%8B%E5%86%8C#fn:2" id="fnref:2" title="See footnote" class="footnote" style="color:red; text-decoration:none; word-wrap:break-word; background:transparent">2</a>,
 你可以使用 Leanote<a target="_blank" href="http://blog.leanote.com/post/freewalk/Markdown-%E8%AF%AD%E6%B3%95%E6%89%8B%E5%86%8C#fn:le" id="fnref:le" title="See footnote" class="footnote" style="color:red; text-decoration:none; word-wrap:break-word; background:transparent">3</a>&nbsp;编辑器进行书写。</p>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
<span style="word-wrap:break-word">注：脚注自动被搬运到最后面，请到文章末尾查看，并且脚注后方的链接可以直接跳转回到加注的地方。</span></p>
<hr style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; height:0px; margin-top:20px; margin-bottom:20px; border-right-width:0px; border-bottom-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; border-top-style:solid; border-top-color:rgb(238,238,238); line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
<h2 id="title-24" style="font-family:&quot;Open Sans&quot;,&quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;,Arial,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:24px; line-height:30px; color:rgb(51,51,51); margin-top:20px; margin-bottom:10px; word-wrap:break-word; font-weight:300!important"><a name="t26"></a>
10. LaTeX 公式</h2>
<h3 id="title-25" style="font-family:&quot;Open Sans&quot;,&quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;,Arial,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; line-height:30px; color:rgb(51,51,51); margin-top:20px; margin-bottom:10px; word-wrap:break-word; font-weight:300!important"><a name="t27"></a>
10.1. $ 表示行内公式：</h3>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
<span style="word-wrap:break-word">代码：</span></p>
<pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted" style="font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,&quot;Courier New&quot;,monospace; font-size:18px; white-space:pre-wrap; padding:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; color:rgb(51,51,51); word-break:break-all; word-wrap:break-word; border:1px solid rgb(225,225,232); background-color:rgb(247,247,249)" name="code"><ol class="linenums" style="margin:0px; word-wrap:break-word; padding:0px 0px 0px 40px"><li class="L0" style="word-wrap:break-word; padding-left:0px; color:rgb(190,190,197)"><code style="font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,&quot;Courier New&quot;,monospace; padding:0px; color:inherit; word-wrap:break-word; background-color:transparent"><span class="pun" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(147,161,161)">质能守恒方程可以用一个很简洁的方程式</span><span class="pln" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(72,72,76)"> $E</span><span class="pun" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(147,161,161)">=</span><span class="pln" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(72,72,76)">mc</span><span class="pun" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(147,161,161)">^</span><span class="lit" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(25,95,145)">2</span><span class="pln" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(72,72,76)">$ </span><span class="pun" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(147,161,161)">来表达。</span></code></li></ol></pre>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
<span style="word-wrap:break-word">显示效果：</span></p>

<h3 id="title-26" style="font-family:&quot;Open Sans&quot;,&quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;,Arial,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; line-height:30px; color:rgb(51,51,51); margin-top:20px; margin-bottom:10px; word-wrap:break-word; font-weight:300!important"><a name="t28"></a>

<h2 id="title-28" style="font-family:&quot;Open Sans&quot;,&quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;,Arial,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:24px; line-height:30px; color:rgb(51,51,51); margin-top:20px; margin-bottom:10px; word-wrap:break-word; font-weight:300!important"><a name="t30"></a>
12 .表格</h2>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
<span style="word-wrap:break-word">语法说明：</span></p>
<ol style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
<li style="word-wrap:break-word">不管是哪种方式，第一行为表头，第二行分隔表头和主体部分，第三行开始每一行为一个表格行。</li><li style="word-wrap:break-word">列于列之间用管道符|隔开。原生方式的表格每一行的两边也要有管道符。</li><li style="word-wrap:break-word">第二行还可以为不同的列指定对齐方向。默认为左对齐，在-右边加上:就右对齐。</li></ol>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
<span style="word-wrap:break-word">代码：</span></p>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">

<h2 id="title-29" style="font-family:&quot;Open Sans&quot;,&quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;,Arial,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:24px; line-height:30px; color:rgb(51,51,51); margin-top:20px; margin-bottom:10px; word-wrap:break-word; font-weight:300!important"><a name="t31"></a>
13. 分隔线</h2>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
你可以在一行中用三个以上的星号、减号、底线来建立一个分隔线，行内不能有其他东西。你也可以在星号或是减号中间插入空格。下面每种写法都可以建立分隔线：</p>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
<span style="word-wrap:break-word">代码：</span></p>
<pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted" style="font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,&quot;Courier New&quot;,monospace; font-size:18px; white-space:pre-wrap; padding:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; padding:0px; color:inherit; word-wrap:break-word; background-color:transparent"><span class="pun" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(147,161,161)">-</span><span class="pln" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(72,72,76)"> </span><span class="pun" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(147,161,161)">-</span><span class="pln" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(72,72,76)"> </span><span class="pun" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(147,161,161)">-</span></code></li><li class="L7" style="word-wrap:break-word; padding-left:0px; color:rgb(190,190,197)"><code style="font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,&quot;Courier New&quot;,monospace; padding:0px; color:inherit; word-wrap:break-word; background-color:transparent"><span class="pun" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(147,161,161)">---------------------------------------</span></code></li></ol></pre>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">

<hr style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; height:0px; margin-top:20px; margin-bottom:20px; border-right-width:0px; border-bottom-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; border-top-style:solid; border-top-color:rgb(238,238,238); line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
<hr style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; height:0px; margin-top:20px; margin-bottom:20px; border-right-width:0px; border-bottom-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; border-top-style:solid; border-top-color:rgb(238,238,238); line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
<h2 id="title-30" style="font-family:&quot;Open Sans&quot;,&quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;,Arial,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:24px; line-height:30px; color:rgb(51,51,51); margin-top:20px; margin-bottom:10px; word-wrap:break-word; font-weight:300!important"><a name="t32"></a>
14. 代码</h2>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
对于程序员来说这个功能是必不可少的，插入程序代码的方式有两种，一种是利用缩进(Tab), 另一种是利用”`”符号（一般在ESC键下方）包裹代码。</p>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
<span style="word-wrap:break-word">语法说明：</span></p>
<ol style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
<li style="word-wrap:break-word">插入行内代码，即插入一个单词或者一句代码的情况，使用`code`这样的形式插入。</li><li style="word-wrap:break-word">插入多行代码，可以使用缩进或者“` code “`,具体看示例。</li></ol>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
<span style="word-wrap:break-word">注意： 缩进式插入前方必须有空行</span></p>
<h3 id="title-31" style="font-family:&quot;Open Sans&quot;,&quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;,Arial,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; line-height:30px; color:rgb(51,51,51); margin-top:20px; margin-bottom:10px; word-wrap:break-word; font-weight:300!important"><a name="t33"></a>
8.1. 行内式</h3>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
<span style="word-wrap:break-word">代码：</span></p>
<pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted" style="font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,&quot;Courier New&quot;,monospace; font-size:18px; white-space:pre-wrap; padding:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; color:rgb(51,51,51); word-break:break-all; word-wrap:break-word; border:1px solid rgb(225,225,232); background-color:rgb(247,247,249)" name="code"><ol class="linenums" style="margin:0px; word-wrap:break-word; padding:0px 0px 0px 40px"><li class="L0" style="word-wrap:break-word; padding-left:0px; color:rgb(190,190,197)"><code style="font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,&quot;Courier New&quot;,monospace; padding:0px; color:inherit; word-wrap:break-word; background-color:transparent"><span class="pln" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(72,72,76)">C</span><span class="pun" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(147,161,161)">语言里的函数</span><span class="pln" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(72,72,76)"> </span><span class="str" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(221,17,68)">`scanf()`</span><span class="pln" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(72,72,76)"> </span><span class="pun" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(147,161,161)">怎么使用？</span></code></li></ol></pre>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
<span style="word-wrap:break-word">显示效果：</span></p>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
C语言里的函数&nbsp;<code style="font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,&quot;Courier New&quot;,monospace; padding:2px 4px; color:rgb(199,37,78); white-space:nowrap; word-wrap:break-word; background-color:rgb(249,242,244)">scanf()</code>&nbsp;怎么使用？</p>
<h3 id="title-32" style="font-family:&quot;Open Sans&quot;,&quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;,Arial,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; line-height:30px; color:rgb(51,51,51); margin-top:20px; margin-bottom:10px; word-wrap:break-word; font-weight:300!important"><a name="t34"></a>
8.2. 缩进式多行代码</h3>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
缩进 4 个空格或是 1 个制表符</p>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
一个代码区块会一直持续到没有缩进的那一行（或是文件结尾）。</p>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
<span style="word-wrap:break-word">代码：</span></p>

<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">

color:rgb(72,72,76)">    printf</span><span class="pun" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(147,161,161)">(</span><span class="str" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(221,17,68)">"Hello world\n"</span><span class="pun" style="word-wrap:break-word; padding:0px; color:inherit; word-wrap:break-word; background-color:transparent"><span class="pun" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(147,161,161)">}</span></code></li></ol></pre>
<h3 id="title-33" style="font-family:&quot;Open Sans&quot;,&quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;,Arial,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; line-height:30px; color:rgb(51,51,51); margin-top:20px; margin-bottom:10px; word-wrap:break-word; font-weight:300!important"><a name="t35"></a>
8.3. 用六个`包裹多行代码</h3>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
<span style="word-wrap:break-word">代码：</span></p>
<pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted" style="font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,&quot;Courier New&quot;,monospace; font-size:18px; white-space:pre-wrap; padding:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; <h3 id="title-34" style="font-family:&quot;Open Sans&quot;,&quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;,Arial,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; line-height:30px; color:rgb(51,51,51); margin-top:20px; margin-bottom:10px; word-wrap:break-word; font-weight:300!important"><a name="t36"></a>
8.4. HTML 原始码</h3>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
在代码区块里面， &amp; 、 &lt; 和 &gt; 会自动转成 HTML 实体，这样的方式让你非常容易使用 Markdown 插入范例用的 HTML 原始码，只需要复制贴上，剩下的 Markdown 都会帮你处理，例如：</p>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
<span style="word-wrap:break-word">代码：</span></p>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
第一个例子：</p>
<pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted" style="font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,&quot;Courier New&quot;,monospace; font-size:18px; white-space:pre-wrap; padding:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; color:rgb(51,51,51); word-break:break-all; word-wrap:break-word; border:1px solid rgb(225,225,232); background-color:rgb(247,247,249)" name="code"><ol class="linenums" style="margin:0px; word-wrap:break-word; padding:0px 0px 0px 40px"><li class="L0" style="word-wrap:break-word; padding-left:0px; color:rgb(190,190,197)"><code style="font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,&quot;Courier New&quot;,monospace; padding:0px; color:inherit; word-wrap:break-word; background-color:transparent"><span class="tag" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(30,52,123)">&lt;div</span><span class="pln" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(72,72,76)"> </span><span class="atn" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(0,128,128)">class</span><span class="pun" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(147,161,161)">=</span><span class="atv" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(221,17,68)">"footer"</span><span class="tag" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(30,52,123)">&gt;</span></code></li><li class="L1" style="word-wrap:break-word; padding-left:0px; color:rgb(190,190,197)"><code style="font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,&quot;Courier New&quot;,monospace; padding:0px; color:inherit; word-wrap:break-word; background-color:transparent"><span class="pln" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(72,72,76)">   © 2004 Foo Corporation</span></code></li><li class="L2" style="word-wrap:break-word; padding-left:0px; color:rgb(190,190,197)"><code style="font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,&quot;Courier New&quot;,monospace; padding:0px; color:inherit; word-wrap:break-word; background-color:transparent"><span class="tag" style="word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(30,52,123)">&lt;/div&gt;</span></code></li></ol></pre>
<p style="font-family:&quot;lucida grande&quot;,&quot;lucida sans unicode&quot;,lucida,helvetica,&quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;,&quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;,&quot;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&quot;,sans-serif; font-size:18px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; line-height:30px; word-wrap:break-word; color:rgb(51,51,51)">
